<span class="token function selector">\textbf</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span>结论：<span class="token punctuation">}</span>FSQ是比VQ更高效、更强大的语音表示方法，是v2性能提升的基石之一。

<span class="token function selector">\subsection*</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span><span class="token headline class-name">2. LLM主干：从自研到预训练（架构简化）</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span>

<span class="token function selector">\begin</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span><span class="token keyword">table</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span>h<span class="token punctuation">]</span>
<span class="token function selector">\centering</span>
<span class="token function selector">\begin</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span><span class="token keyword">tabular</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span>p<span class="token punctuation">{</span>0.45<span class="token function selector">\textwidth</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span>p<span class="token punctuation">{</span>0.45<span class="token function selector">\textwidth</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
<span class="token function selector">\toprule</span>
<span class="token function selector">\textbf</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span>CosyVoice<span class="token punctuation">}</span> <span class="token punctuation">&amp;</span> <span class="token function selector">\textbf</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span>CosyVoice 2<span class="token punctuation">}</span> <span class="token function selector">\\</span>
<span class="token function selector">\midrule</span>
• 包含专门的文本编码器对齐语义空间 <span class="token punctuation">&amp;</span> • 移除文本编码器：直接使用原始文本BPE标记 <span class="token function selector">\\</span>
<span class="token function selector">\rowcolor</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span>lightgray<span class="token punctuation">}</span>
• 输入中包含说话人嵌入，可能导致信息泄漏 <span class="token punctuation">&amp;</span> • 移除说话人嵌入：依赖预训练LLM（Qwen2.5）自行完成对齐 <span class="token function selector">\\</span>
• 干扰模型对纯内容的学习 <span class="token punctuation">&amp;</span> • 让LLM专注于学习语义内容 <span class="token function selector">\\</span>
<span class="token function selector">\bottomrule</span>
<span class="token function selector">\end</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span><span class="token keyword">tabular</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
<span class="token function selector">\end</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span><span class="token keyword">table</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span>

<span class="token function selector">\textbf</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span>结论：<span class="token punctuation">}</span>这种职责分离的设计更清晰：LLM管"说什么"，流匹配模型管"怎么说、谁来说"。简化架构带来内容一致性大幅提升（CER从3.63\<span class="token comment">%降至1.45\%）和更好的跨语言能力。</span>

<span class="token function selector">\subsection*</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span><span class="token headline class-name">3. 声学模型：从非流式到流式统一（范式突破）</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span>

<span class="token function selector">\begin</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span><span class="token keyword">table</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span>h<span class="token punctuation">]</span>
<span class="token function selector">\centering</span>
<span class="token function selector">\begin</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span><span class="token keyword">tabular</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span>p<span class="token punctuation">{</span>0.45<span class="token function selector">\textwidth</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span>p<span class="token punctuation">{</span>0.45<span class="token function selector">\textwidth</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
<span class="token function selector">\toprule</span>
<span class="token function selector">\textbf</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span>CosyVoice<span class="token punctuation">}</span> <span class="token punctuation">&amp;</span> <span class="token function selector">\textbf</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span>CosyVoice 2<span class="token punctuation">}</span> <span class="token function selector">\\</span>
<span class="token function selector">\midrule</span>
<span class="token function selector">\textbf</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span>标准流匹配模型：<span class="token punctuation">}</span> <span class="token punctuation">&amp;</span> <span class="token function selector">\textbf</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span>块感知因果流匹配：<span class="token punctuation">}</span> <span class="token function selector">\\</span>
• 需要整个语音标记序列生成梅尔频谱图 <span class="token punctuation">&amp;</span> • <span class="token function selector">\textbf</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span>核心创新：<span class="token punctuation">}</span>引入四种注意力掩码 <span class="token function selector">\\</span>
• 仅支持非流式 <span class="token punctuation">&amp;</span> - 非因果、全因果、Chunk-M, Chunk-2M <span class="token function selector">\\</span>
<span class="token function selector">\rowcolor</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span>lightgray<span class="token punctuation">}</span>
<span class="token punctuation">&amp;</span> • 训练时学会在不同上下文限制下生成高质量语音 <span class="token function selector">\\</span>
<span class="token punctuation">&amp;</span> <span class="token function selector">\textbf</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span>结果：<span class="token punctuation">}</span>单一模型支持多种模式： <span class="token function selector">\\</span>
<span class="token punctuation">&amp;</span> - 追求质量：非流式 <span class="token function selector">\\</span>
<span class="token punctuation">&amp;</span> - 最低延迟：全流式 <span class="token function selector">\\</span>
<span class="token punctuation">&amp;</span> - 质量延迟权衡：块流式 <span class="token function selector">\\</span>
<span class="token function selector">\bottomrule</span>
<span class="token function selector">\end</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span><span class="token keyword">tabular</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
<span class="token function selector">\end</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span><span class="token keyword">table</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span>

<span class="token function selector">\textbf</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span>结论：<span class="token punctuation">}</span>这是工程上的巨大进步，解决了高质量TTS模型无法流式合成的行业难题，使CosyVoice 2能够应用于实时语音聊天等场景。

<span class="token function selector">\subsection*</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span><span class="token headline class-name">4. 合成质量指标对比</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span>

<span class="token function selector">\begin</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span><span class="token keyword">table</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span>h<span class="token punctuation">]</span>
<span class="token function selector">\centering</span>
<span class="token function selector">\begin</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span><span class="token keyword">tabular</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span>lccc<span class="token punctuation">}</span>
<span class="token function selector">\toprule</span>
<span class="token function selector">\textbf</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span>指标<span class="token punctuation">}</span> <span class="token punctuation">&amp;</span> <span class="token function selector">\textbf</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span>CosyVoice (v1)<span class="token punctuation">}</span> <span class="token punctuation">&amp;</span> <span class="token function selector">\textbf</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span>CosyVoice 2 (v2)<span class="token punctuation">}</span> <span class="token punctuation">&amp;</span> <span class="token function selector">\textbf</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span>改进幅度<span class="token punctuation">}</span> <span class="token function selector">\\</span>
<span class="token function selector">\midrule</span>
<span class="token function selector">\textbf</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span>内容一致性 (CER)<span class="token punctuation">}</span> <span class="token punctuation">&amp;</span> 3.63\<span class="token comment">% &amp; 1.45\% &amp; \textcolor{red}{$\downarrow$ 60\%} \\</span>
<span class="token function selector">\textbf</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span>说话人相似度 (SS)<span class="token punctuation">}</span> <span class="token punctuation">&amp;</span> 优秀 <span class="token punctuation">&amp;</span> 持平或略优 <span class="token punctuation">&amp;</span> <span class="token equation string">$<span class="token equation-command regex">\rightarrow</span>$</span> <span class="token function selector">\\</span>
<span class="token function selector">\textbf</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span>语音自然度 (NMOS)<span class="token punctuation">}</span> <span class="token punctuation">&amp;</span> 3.93 <span class="token punctuation">&amp;</span> 3.96 <span class="token punctuation">&amp;</span> <span class="token equation string">$<span class="token equation-command regex">\uparrow</span>$</span> <span class="token function selector">\\</span>
<span class="token function selector">\rowcolor</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span>lightgray<span class="token punctuation">}</span>
<span class="token function selector">\textbf</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span>流式合成质量<span class="token punctuation">}</span> <span class="token punctuation">&amp;</span> 不支持 <span class="token punctuation">&amp;</span> 近乎无损 <span class="token punctuation">&amp;</span> <span class="token function selector">\textcolor</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span>red<span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span><span class="token equation string">$<span class="token equation-command regex">\uparrow</span>$</span> 突破性<span class="token punctuation">}</span> <span class="token function selector">\\</span>
<span class="token function selector">\textbf</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span>多语言能力<span class="token punctuation">}</span> <span class="token punctuation">&amp;</span> 支持 <span class="token punctuation">&amp;</span> 零样本能力更强 <span class="token punctuation">&amp;</span> <span class="token equation string">$<span class="token equation-command regex">\uparrow</span>$</span> <span class="token function selector">\\</span>
<span class="token function selector">\bottomrule</span>
<span class="token function selector">\end</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span><span class="token keyword">tabular</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
<span class="token function selector">\end</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span><span class="token keyword">table</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span>

<span class="token function selector">\textbf</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span>总结：<span class="token punctuation">}</span>CosyVoice 2在几乎所有方面都是CosyVoice的全面升级和超越，特别是在流式合成这一关键能力上实现了从0到1的突破。
